			}
		}

		cost = 0

				is_faction_leader = yes

			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision BRG_join_CRAIC_decision target: [From.GetName]"

				if = {
					limit = {

						NOT = { has_idea = BRG_commonwealth_member_idea }
					}
				}
				add_ideas = BRG_commonwealth_member_idea
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
